Header file for the CUDA Toolkit application programming interface.

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{cuDeviceGetExecAffinitySupport()}{cuDeviceGetExecAffinitySupport()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gaf18c3affd9d913e337e3794abeade307}{CUresult}} CUDAAPI cu\+Device\+Get\+Exec\+Affinity\+Support (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{int}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{pi,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_gad4bcf6bf1598b9274657d452efbbd262}{CUexec\+Affinity\+Type}}}]{type,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{group___c_u_d_a___t_y_p_e_s_ga41ca2a24a242b36ef2ca77330b5fb72a}{CUdevice}}}]{dev }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Returns information about the execution affinity support of the device. 

Returns in {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}pi} whether execution affinity type {\ttfamily type} is supported by device {\ttfamily dev}. The supported types are\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \doxylink{group___c_u_d_a_r_t___t_e_x_t_u_r_e___o_b_j_e_c_t_ga91840d654e4a4ffb86e9b2fd793e9196}{CU\+\_\+\+EXEC\+\_\+\+AFFINITY\+\_\+\+TYPE\+\_\+\+SM\+\_\+\+COUNT\+:} 1 if context with limited SMs is supported by the device, or 0 if not;
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em pi} & -\/ 1 if the execution affinity type {\ttfamily type} is supported by the device, or 0 if not \\
\hline
{\em type} & -\/ Execution affinity type to query \\
\hline
{\em dev} & -\/ Device handle\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
